export function FloatingAIAssistant() {
  const location = useLocation();
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<TabKey>('数据');

            initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 20 }}

            exit={{ opacity: 0, x: 20 }}
            className="fixed right-0 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 z-40"
          >
            <button
              onClick={() => setOpen(true)}
              className="flex flex-col items-center gap-1 bg-primary text-primary-foreground px-2 py-4 rounded-l-xl shadow-lg hover:opacity-90 transition-opacity"
            >
              <Bot className="w-5 h-5" />

            </button>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>

        {open && (

            <motion.div
              initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
              className="fixed inset-0 z-40 bg-black/20 backdrop-blur-[1px] md:hidden"

export default function SettingsPage() {
  const { profile } = useAuth();
  const [saved, setSaved] = useState(false);
  const [selectedAvatar, setSelectedAvatar] = useState<string>('');
  const [uploadedAvatar, setUploadedAvatar] = useState<string>('');
  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
  const [notifications, setNotifications] = useState({
    email: true, sms: false, push: true, dailyReport: true, weeklyDigest: false,
  });
  const [profileForm, setProfileForm] = useState({
    display_name: profile?.display_name || '',
    department: profile?.department || '',
    region: profile?.region || '',
  });

  const currentAvatar = uploadedAvatar || selectedAvatar;

  const handleAvatarUpload = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const file = e.target.files?.[0];
    if (!file) return;
    if (!file.type.startsWith('image/')) { toast.error('请上传图片格式文件'); return; }
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = (ev) => {
      setUploadedAvatar(ev.target?.result as string);
      setSelectedAvatar('');
      toast.success('头像已更新');
    };
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    e.target.value = '';
  };

  const handleSave = () => {
    setSaved(true);
    toast.success('设置已保存');
    setTimeout(() => setSaved(false), 2000);
  };

  return (
    <AppLayout title="个人中心">
      <div className="p-4 md:p-6 max-w-3xl mx-auto">
        <Tabs defaultValue="profile" className="w-full">
          <TabsList className="rounded-sm mb-6 flex flex-wrap h-auto gap-1">
            <TabsTrigger value="profile" className="rounded-sm text-xs gap-1.5"><User className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />个人资料</TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="notifications" className="rounded-sm text-xs gap-1.5"><Bell className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />通知设置</TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="security" className="rounded-sm text-xs gap-1.5"><Shield className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />账号安全</TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="appearance" className="rounded-sm text-xs gap-1.5"><Palette className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />界面偏好</TabsTrigger>
          </TabsList>

          {/* 个人资料 */}
          <TabsContent value="profile">
            <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 12 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}>
              <Card className="rounded-sm border-border shadow-sm">
                <CardHeader className="pb-4">
                  <CardTitle className="text-sm font-semibold">个人资料</CardTitle>
                </CardHeader>
                <CardContent className="space-y-5">
                  {/* 头像区域 */}
                  <div className="space-y-4">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
                      <Avatar className="w-16 h-16 ring-2 ring-primary/20">
                        <AvatarImage src={currentAvatar} className="object-cover" />
                        <AvatarFallback className="text-xl bg-primary text-primary-foreground">
                          {(profile?.display_name || profile?.username || '用')?.slice(0, 1)}
                        </AvatarFallback>
                      </Avatar>
                      <div>
                        <p className="text-sm font-medium">{profile?.display_name || profile?.username || '未设置昵称'}</p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">
                          {profile?.role === 'admin' ? '管理员' : profile?.role === 'manager' ? '运营经理' : '运营顾问'}
                        </p>
                        <input ref={fileInputRef} type="file" accept="image/*" className="hidden" onChange={handleAvatarUpload} />
                        <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="mt-2 rounded-sm text-xs h-7" onClick={() => fileInputRef.current?.click()}>
                          <Upload className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" /> 上传头像
                        </Button>
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    {/* 内置女生头像选择 */}
                    <div className="space-y-2">
                      <p className="text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground">选择内置头像</p>
                      <div className="grid grid-cols-5 gap-2">
                        {BUILTIN_AVATARS.map(av => (
                          <button
                            key={av.id}
                            onClick={() => { setSelectedAvatar(av.url); setUploadedAvatar(''); }}
                            className={`relative rounded-sm overflow-hidden aspect-square border-2 transition-all hover:scale-105 ${
                              selectedAvatar === av.url ? 'border-primary ring-2 ring-primary/30' : 'border-border'
                            }`}
                          >
                            <img src={av.url} alt={av.label} className="w-full h-full object-cover" />
                            {selectedAvatar === av.url && (
                              <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-primary/20 flex items-center justify-center">
                                <CheckCircle2 className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />
                              </div>
                            )}
                          </button>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                      <div className="grid grid-cols-5 gap-2">
                        {BUILTIN_AVATARS.map(av => (
                          <p key={av.id} className="text-[10px] text-center text-muted-foreground truncate">{av.label}</p>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>

const defaultAnalysis: AnalysisResult = getAIAnalysis('other');

export function FloatingAIAssistant() {
  const location = useLocation();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [analysis, setAnalysis] = useState(defaultAnalysis);
  const [expandedInsight, setExpandedInsight] = useState<number | null>(null);

  const pageType = detectPageType(location.pathname);

  // 不在 landing/login 页显示
  const hidden = ['/landing', '/login'].includes(location.pathname);
  if (hidden) return null;

  const refresh = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 900));
    setAnalysis(getAIAnalysis(pageType));
    setLoading(false);
    toast.success('AI 分析已更新');
  }, [pageType]);

  // 切换页面时自动更新分析
  useEffect(() => {
    setAnalysis(getAIAnalysis(pageType));
    setExpandedInsight(null);
  }, [pageType]);

// 页面类型识别
type PageType = 'home' | 'merchant-detail' | 'merchants' | 'communications' | 'data-center' | 'other';

function detectPageType(pathname: string): PageType {
  if (pathname.startsWith('/merchant/')) return 'merchant-detail';
  if (pathname === '/') return 'home';
  if (pathname.startsWith('/merchants')) return 'merchants';
  if (pathname.startsWith('/communications')) return 'communications';
  if (pathname.startsWith('/data-center')) return 'data-center';
  return 'other';
}

    81 function AnimatedCounter({ target, suffix }: { target: number; suffix: string }) {
    82   const [count, setCount] = useState(0);
    83   const ref = useRef<HTMLSpanElement>(null);
    84   const started = useRef(false);
    85 
    86   useEffect(() => {
    87     const observer = new IntersectionObserver(([entry]) => {
    88       if (entry.isIntersecting && !started.current) {
    89         started.current = true;
    90         const duration = 1800;
    91         const start = performance.now();
    92         const tick = (now: number) => {
    93           const progress = Math.min((now - start) / duration, 1);
    94           const eased = 1 - Math.pow(1 - progress, 3);
    95           setCount(Math.round(eased * target));
    96           if (progress < 1) requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    97         };
    98         requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    99       }
   100     }, { threshold: 0.5 });

   108 function FloatingCard3D({ children, delay = 0 }: { children: React.ReactNode; delay?: number }) {
   109   const x = useMotionValue(0);
   110   const y = useMotionValue(0);
   111   const rotateX = useSpring(useTransform(y, [-50, 50], [8, -8]), { stiffness: 300, damping: 30 });
   112   const rotateY = useSpring(useTransform(x, [-50, 50], [-8, 8]), { stiffness: 300, damping: 30 });
   113 
   114   return (
   115     <motion.div
   116       style={{ rotateX, rotateY, transformStyle: 'preserve-3d', perspective: 800 }}
   117       initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 30 }}
   118       whileInView={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
   119       viewport={{ once: true }}
   120       transition={{ duration: 0.6, delay }}
   121       onMouseMove={e => {
   122         const rect = (e.currentTarget as HTMLElement).getBoundingClientRect();
   123         x.set(e.clientX - rect.left - rect.width / 2);
   124         y.set(e.clientY - rect.top - rect.height / 2);
   125       }}
   126       onMouseLeave={() => { x.set(0); y.set(0); }}
   127       className="cursor-pointer"
   128     >
   129       {children}
   130     </motion.div>
   131   );
   132 }

   288 export function getMockMerchantList(params?: {
   289   count?: number;
   290   filters?: { category?: string; level?: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low' };
   291 }): MerchantListItem[] {
   292   const count = params?.count ?? 50;
   293   const list: MerchantListItem[] = [];
   294 
   295   for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   296     const id = `m-${1000 + i}`;
   297     const category = ['餐饮', '丽人', '休闲娱乐', '酒店旅游', '亲子教育', '运动健身', '生活服务', '医疗健康'][i % 8];
   298     const monthlySales = Math.round(30000 + Math.random() * 150000);
   299     const monthlyOrders = Math.round(monthlySales / (40 + Math.random() * 50));
   300     const connectionRate = Math.round(40 + Math.random() * 55);
   301 
   302     const merchant = getMockMerchantById(id);
   303     const level = merchant.acceptancePrediction.level;
   304 
   305     if (params?.filters?.category && params.filters.category !== category) continue;
   306     if (params?.filters?.level && params.filters.level !== level) continue;
   307 
   308     const advantageTags: string[] = [];
   309     if (monthlySales > 80000) advantageTags.push('高流水');
   310     if (connectionRate > 75) advantageTags.push('易接通');
   311     if (level === 'high') advantageTags.push('高意向');
   312     if (merchant.operationData.rating > 4.3) advantageTags.push('好评店');
   313     if (advantageTags.length === 0) advantageTags.push('潜力门店');
   314 
   315     const seasonPotential: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low' = merchant.benchmark.seasonFactor > 1.1 ? 'high' : merchant.benchmark.seasonFactor > 0.9 ? 'medium' : 'low';
   316 
   317     list.push({
   318       id,
   319       name: merchant.basicInfo.name,
   320       category,
   321       monthlySales,
   322       monthlyOrders,
   323       connectionRate,
   324       acceptanceLevel: level,
   325       potentialScore: Math.round(
   326         (monthlySales / 2000) * 0.3 +
   327         connectionRate * 0.4 +
   328         (merchant.benchmark.seasonFactor - 0.5) * 30 +
   329         (level === 'high' ? 20 : level === 'medium' ? 10 : 0)
   330       ),
   331       advantageTags,
   332       seasonPotential,
   333       avatarUrl: MERCHANT_AVATARS[Math.abs(merchant.basicInfo.name.charCodeAt(0) + merchant.basicInfo.name.charCodeAt(1)) % MERCHANT_AVATARS.length],
   334       address: merchant.basicInfo.address,
   335       contactPhone: merchant.basicInfo.contactPhone,
   336       managerName: merchant.basicInfo.managerName,
   337     });
   338   }
   339 
   340   return list.sort((a, b) => b.potentialScore - a.potentialScore);
   341 }
   342 
   343 export function filterMockMerchantList(
   344   list: MerchantListItem[],
   345   filters: {
   346     salesMin?: number;
   347     salesMax?: number;
   348     category?: string;
   349     connectionRateMin?: number;
   350     acceptanceLevel?: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low';
   351     seasonPotential?: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low';
   352     keyword?: string;
   353   }
   354 ): MerchantListItem[] {
   355   return list.filter((item) => {
   356     if (filters.salesMin !== undefined && item.monthlySales < filters.salesMin) return false;
   357     if (filters.salesMax !== undefined && item.monthlySales > filters.salesMax) return false;
   358     if (filters.category && item.category !== filters.category) return false;
   359     if (filters.connectionRateMin !== undefined && item.connectionRate < filters.connectionRateMin) return false;
   360     if (filters.acceptanceLevel && item.acceptanceLevel !== filters.acceptanceLevel) return false;

export function getMockMerchantList(params?: {
  count?: number;
  filters?: { category?: string; level?: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low' };
}): MerchantListItem[] {
  const count = params?.count ?? 50;
  const list: MerchantListItem[] = [];

  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const id = `m-${1000 + i}`;
    const category = ['餐饮', '丽人', '休闲娱乐', '酒店旅游', '亲子教育', '运动健身', '生活服务', '医疗健康'][i % 8];
    const monthlySales = Math.round(30000 + Math.random() * 150000);
    const monthlyOrders = Math.round(monthlySales / (40 + Math.random() * 50));
    const connectionRate = Math.round(40 + Math.random() * 55);

    const merchant = getMockMerchantById(id);
    const level = merchant.acceptancePrediction.level;

    if (params?.filters?.category && params.filters.category !== category) continue;
    if (params?.filters?.level && params.filters.level !== level) continue;

    const advantageTags: string[] = [];
    if (monthlySales > 80000) advantageTags.push('高流水');
    if (connectionRate > 75) advantageTags.push('易接通');
    if (level === 'high') advantageTags.push('高意向');
    if (merchant.operationData.rating > 4.3) advantageTags.push('好评店');
    if (advantageTags.length === 0) advantageTags.push('潜力门店');

    const seasonPotential: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low' = merchant.benchmark.seasonFactor > 1.1 ? 'high' : merchant.benchmark.seasonFactor > 0.9 ? 'medium' : 'low';

    list.push({
      id,
      name: merchant.basicInfo.name,
      category,
      monthlySales,
      monthlyOrders,
      connectionRate,
      acceptanceLevel: level,
      potentialScore: Math.round(
        (monthlySales / 2000) * 0.3 +
        connectionRate * 0.4 +
        (merchant.benchmark.seasonFactor - 0.5) * 30 +
        (level === 'high' ? 20 : level === 'medium' ? 10 : 0)
      ),
      advantageTags,
      seasonPotential,
      avatarUrl: MERCHANT_AVATARS[Math.abs(merchant.basicInfo.name.charCodeAt(0) + merchant.basicInfo.name.charCodeAt(1)) % MERCHANT_AVATARS.length],
      address: merchant.basicInfo.address,
      contactPhone: merchant.basicInfo.contactPhone,
      managerName: merchant.basicInfo.managerName,
    });
  }

  return list.sort((a, b) => b.potentialScore - a.potentialScore);
}

    71 export function FloatingAIAssistant() {
    72   const location = useLocation();
    73   const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
    74   const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<TabKey>('数据');
    75 
    76   const hidden = ['/landing', '/login'].includes(location.pathname);
    77   if (hidden) return null;
    78 
    79   return (
    80     <>
    81       {/* 触发按钮 */}
    82       <AnimatePresence>
    83         {!open && (
    84           <motion.div
    85             initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 20 }}
    86             animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
    87             exit={{ opacity: 0, x: 20 }}
    88             className="fixed right-0 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 z-40"
    89           >
    90             <button
    91               onClick={() => setOpen(true)}
    92               className="flex flex-col items-center gap-1 bg-primary text-primary-foreground px-2 py-4 rounded-l-xl shadow-lg hover:opacity-90 transition-opacity"
    93             >
    94               <Bot className="w-5 h-5" />
    95               <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold" style={{ writingMode: 'vertical-rl', letterSpacing: '0.1em' }}>AI 助手</span>
    96               <ChevronLeft className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mt-1" />
    97             </button>
    98           </motion.div>
    99         )}
   100       </AnimatePresence>
   101 
   102       {/* 侧边面板 */}
   103       <AnimatePresence>
   104         {open && (
   105           <>
   106             <motion.div
   107               initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
   108               className="fixed inset-0 z-40 bg-black/20 backdrop-blur-[1px] md:hidden"
   109               onClick={() => setOpen(false)}
   110             />
   111             <motion.div
   112               initial={{ x: '100%' }} animate={{ x: 0 }} exit={{ x: '100%' }}
   113               transition={{ type: 'spring', stiffness: 280, damping: 30 }}
   114               className="fixed right-0 top-0 bottom-0 z-50 w-80 md:w-[360px] bg-card border-l border-border shadow-2xl flex flex-col"
   115             >
   116               {/* 头部 */}
   117               <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-border bg-primary text-primary-foreground shrink-0">
   118                 <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   119                   <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded-sm bg-primary-foreground/20 flex items-center justify-center">
   120                     <Bot className="w-4 h-4" />
   121                   </div>
   122                   <div>
   123                     <h2 className="font-semibold text-sm">AI 运营助手</h2>
   124                     <p className="text-[10px] opacity-70">美团阿波罗智能插件</p>
   125                   </div>
   126                 </div>
   127                 <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-7 w-7 rounded-sm text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary-foreground/10" onClick={() => setOpen(false)}>
   128                   <X className="w-4 h-4" />
   129                 </Button>
   130               </div>
   131 
   132               {/* Tab 导航 */}
   133               <Tabs value={activeTab} onValueChange={v => setActiveTab(v as TabKey)} className="flex-1 flex flex-col min-h-0">
   134                 <TabsList className="grid grid-cols-5 h-9 rounded-none border-b border-border bg-muted/40 shrink-0 px-1">
   135                   {(Object.keys(TAB_DATA) as TabKey[]).map(tab => (
   136                     <TabsTrigger key={tab} value={tab} className="text-[11px] rounded-sm data-[state=active]:bg-background data-[state=active]:shadow-sm px-1">
   137                       {tab}
   138                     </TabsTrigger>
   139                   ))}
   140                 </TabsList>
   141 
   142                 <ScrollArea className="flex-1 min-h-0">
   143                   {/* 数据 Tab */}
   144                   <TabsContent value="数据" className="m-0 p-4 space-y-3">
   145                     <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">{TAB_DATA['数据'].summary}</p>
   146                     <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
   147                       {TAB_DATA['数据'].metrics.map(m => (
   148                         <div key={m.label} className="rounded-sm border border-border bg-background p-2.5">
   149                           <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{m.label}</p>
   150                           <p className="text-sm font-bold mt-0.5">{m.value}</p>
   151                           <p className={`text-[10px] font-medium ${m.up ? 'text-success' : 'text-destructive'}`}>{m.change}</p>
   152                         </div>
   153                       ))}
   154                     </div>
   155                   </TabsContent>
   156 
   157                   {/* 诊断 Tab */}

   168                   </TabsContent>
   169

   187   const [records, setRecords] = useState<CommRecord[]>(() => genMockComms());

   196   const [form, setForm]         = useState(EMPTY_FORM);
   197 
   198   const [followUps, setFollowUps] = useState<FollowUpItem[]>(genInitialFollowUps);
   199   const [fuAddOpen, setFuAddOpen] = useState(false);
   200   const [fuForm, setFuForm]       = useState({ name: '', time: '', priority: 'medium', reason: '' });
   201   const [fuDeleteId, setFuDeleteId] = useState<string | null>(null);
   202   const [fuEditTarget, setFuEditTarget] = useState<FollowUpItem | null>(null);
   203 
   204   const filtered = useMemo(() => records.filter(r => {
   205     if (keyword && !r.merchant_name.includes(keyword) && !r.content.includes(keyword)) return false;
   206     if (channel !== 'all' && r.channel !== channel) return false;
   207     if (result  !== 'all' && r.result  !== result)  return false;
   208     return true;
   209   }), [records, keyword, channel, result]);
   210 
   211   const pendingFollowUps = followUps.filter(f => !f.done);
   212 
   213   // ── 沟通记录 CRUD ──
   214   const handleAddRecord = () => {
   215     if (!form.merchant.trim() || !form.content.trim()) { toast.error('请填写商家和沟通内容'); return; }
   216     const newRec: CommRecord = {
   217       id: `comm-new-${Date.now()}`,
   218       merchant_name: form.merchant,
   219       channel: form.channel as CommRecord['channel'],
   220       duration_minutes: form.duration ? Number(form.duration) : null,
   221       content: form.content,
   222       result: form.result as CommRecord['result'],
   223       contact_time: new Date().toISOString(),
   224       operator: '当前用户',
   225     };
   226     setRecords(prev => [newRec, ...prev]);
   227     toast.success('沟通记录已保存');
   228     setAddOpen(false);
   229     setForm(EMPTY_FORM);
   230   };
   231 
   232   const handleEditRecord = () => {
   233     if (!editRecord || !form.merchant.trim() || !form.content.trim()) { toast.error('请填写商家和沟通内容'); return; }
   234     setRecords(prev => prev.map(r => r.id === editRecord.id
   235       ? { ...r, merchant_name: form.merchant, channel: form.channel as CommRecord['channel'], content: form.content, result: form.result as CommRecord['result'], duration_minutes: form.duration ? Number(form.duration) : null }
   236       : r
   237     ));
   238     toast.success('记录已更新');
   239     setEditRecord(null);
   240     setForm(EMPTY_FORM);
   241   };
   242 
   243   const openEdit = (r: CommRecord) => {
   244     setEditRecord(r);
   245     setForm({ merchant: r.merchant_name, channel: r.channel, content: r.content, result: r.result, duration: String(r.duration_minutes ?? '') });
   246   };
   247 
   248   // ── 待跟进 CRUD ──
   249   const handleAddFu = () => {
   250     if (!fuForm.name.trim()) { toast.error('请输入商家名称'); return; }
   251     setFollowUps(prev => [...prev, { id: `fu-${Date.now()}`, name: fuForm.name, time: fuForm.time || '待定', priority: fuForm.priority as 'high'|'medium'|'low', reason: fuForm.reason, done: false }]);
   252     toast.success('待跟进任务已添加');
   253     setFuAddOpen(false);
   254     setFuForm({ name: '', time: '', priority: 'medium', reason: '' });
   255   };
   256 
   257   const handleEditFu = () => {
   258     if (!fuEditTarget) return;
   259     setFollowUps(prev => prev.map(f => f.id === fuEditTarget.id ? { ...f, name: fuForm.name, time: fuForm.time, priority: fuForm.priority as 'high'|'medium'|'low', reason: fuForm.reason } : f));
   260     toast.success('跟进任务已更新');
   261     setFuEditTarget(null);
   262     setFuForm({ name: '', time: '', priority: 'medium', reason: '' });
   263   };
   264 
   265   return (
   266     <AppLayout title="沟通记录" actions={
   267       <Button size="sm" className="rounded-sm text-xs" onClick={() => { setForm(EMPTY_FORM); setAddOpen(true); }}>
   268         <Plus className="w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-1" />记录沟通

function KangarooAdvisor() {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<ChatMessage[]>([]);
  const [inputText, setInputText] = useState('');
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false);
  const scrollRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);

  const scrollToBottom = () => {
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (scrollRef.current) scrollRef.current.scrollTop = scrollRef.current.scrollHeight;
    }, 100);
  };

  const sendMessage = useCallback((text: string) => {
    if (!text.trim()) return;
    const userMsg: ChatMessage = { id: `u-${Date.now()}`, role: 'user', text };
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, userMsg]);
    setInputText('');
    setIsTyping(true);
    scrollToBottom();

    setTimeout(() => {
      const matchKey = Object.keys(MOCK_ANSWERS).find(k => text.includes(k));
      const replyText = matchKey ? MOCK_ANSWERS[matchKey] : `感谢您的提问！关于"${text}"，袋鼠参谋正在为您分析最新行业数据，结合美团平台实时数据与AI模型，为您提供专属经营建议。建议您可以从市场需求、竞争格局和门店运营三个维度综合考量，如需详细报告可点击下方「数据报告」获取完整分析。`;
      const assistantMsg: ChatMessage = { id: `a-${Date.now()}`, role: 'assistant', text: replyText };
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, assistantMsg]);
      setIsTyping(false);
      scrollToBottom();
    }, 1200);
  }, []);

  const showWelcome = messages.length === 0;

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-full min-h-0" style={{ height: 'calc(100vh - 180px)', minHeight: 520 }}>

                  <ellipse cx="52" cy="14" rx="5" ry="8" fill="#F5C842" transform="rotate(20 52 14)"/>
                  <ellipse cx="29" cy="17" rx="2.5" ry="5" fill="#E8A0A0" transform="rotate(-20 29 17)"/>
                  <ellipse cx="51" cy="15" rx="2.5" ry="5" fill="#E8A0A0" transform="rotate(20 51 15)"/>

                  <rect x="28" y="14" width="24" height="4" rx="2" fill="#555"/>

            value={inputText}
            onChange={e => setInputText(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={e => { if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) { e.preventDefault(); sendMessage(inputText); } }}
            placeholder="有问题随时问我..."

              <ImageIcon className="w-4 h-4" />

            <button className="w-7 h-7 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground hover:bg-background transition-colors" onClick={() => toast.info('文件上传即将上线')}>

              onClick={() => sendMessage(inputText)}

            >
              <SendHorizonal className="w-4 h-4" />

        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-2 px-1">
          {[{ icon: Zap, label: 'AI营销诊断' }, { icon: BarChart2, label: '数据解读' }, { icon: MapPin, label: '选址建议' }, { icon: Utensils, label: '菜品研发' }].map(chip => (

              <chip.icon className="w-3 h-3" />{chip.label}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
